   A) वायु की गुणवत्ता संवेदनशील समूहों के स्वास्थ्य पर प्रतिकूल प्रभाव डाल सकती है  <-- CORRECT
   B) वायु की गुणवत्ता उत्कृष्ट है
   C) वायु की गुणवत्ता संतोषजनक है
   D) वायु की गुणवत्ता सभी के लिए खतरनाक है
Answer: A
Why correct: In the Air Quality Index, the 'Moderate' category indicates that air quality may adversely affect the health of sensitive groups (such as people with respiratory issues).
Why B is wrong: 'Good' (not Moderate) means excellent air quality.

Set 13 | Q.No 27 | Topic: Science & Technology | Language: Hindi
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Q: भूस्थिरीय कक्ष में एक उपग्रह, पृथ्वी की भूमध्य रेखा (६५७०६०) पर किसी बिंदु के ऊपर स्थिर रहता है। उपग्रह की अक्षीय त्रिज्या लगभग 42,200 किमी है। उपग्रह की कक्षीय अवधि घंटे में परिकलित कीजिए।
   A) 24 घंटे  <-- CORRECT
   B) 12 de
   C) 6 घंटे
   D) 48 घंटे
Answer: A
Why correct: A geostationary satellite stays fixed above a point on the equator, which requires an orbital period equal to the Earth's rotation - about 24 hours.
Why B is wrong: 12 hours corresponds to a lower (e.g. GPS-type) orbit.
Why C is wrong: 6 hours is far too short for geostationary orbit.
Why D is wrong: 48 hours is twice the Earth's rotation period.
Note: Geostationary satellites orbit at about 35,786 km above the equator and are widely used for communication and weather monitoring.

Set 14 | Q.No 22 | Topic: Science & Technology | Language: Hindi
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Q: मुक्त गिरावट के दौरान (वायु प्रतिरोध की उपेक्षा करते हुए) किसी वस्तु के जमीन से टकराने से ठीक पहले, उसकी स्थितिज और गतिज ऊर्जाएं किस प्रकार संबंधित होती हैं?
   A) स्थितिज ऊर्जा अधिकतम है, गतिज ऊर्जा न्यूनतम है
   B) स्थितिज ऊर्जा न्यूनतम, गतिज ऊर्जा अधिकतम  <-- CORRECT
   C) गतिज और स्थितिज ऊर्जा दोनों शून्य हैं
   D) परिवर्तन के कारण कुछ ऊर्जा नष्ट हो जाती है
Answer: B
Why correct: In free fall (ignoring air resistance), just before hitting the ground the object's potential energy is at a minimum and its kinetic energy is at a maximum, as PE converts into KE.
Why A is wrong: PE is minimum (not maximum) at the lowest point.
Why C is wrong: Both energies are not zero; KE is maximum.
Why D is wrong: In ideal free fall total mechanical energy is conserved, so no energy is lost.
Note: This illustrates conservation of mechanical energy: PE + KE remains constant throughout the fall.

Set 14 | Q.No 25 | Topic: Science & Technology | Language: Hindi

Q: यदि उपग्रह की कक्षीय अवधि 90 मिनट है, तो उसे कक्षा में बनाए रखने वाला प्रमुख बल क्या होगा?
   A) पृथ्वी का गुरुत्वाकर्षण बल  <-- CORRECT
   B) उपग्रह का अपकेंद्री बल
   C) पृथ्वी से चुंबकीय बल
   D) विद्युत चुंबकीय बल
Answer: A
Why correct: The main force that keeps a satellite in orbit (period 90 minutes) is the Earth's gravitational force, which provides the necessary centripetal force.
Why B is wrong: The 'centrifugal force' is a pseudo-force in the rotating frame, not the real force holding the satellite.
Why C is wrong: Earth's magnetic force is far too weak to hold a satellite in orbit.
Why D is wrong: Electromagnetic force is not what keeps a satellite orbiting.
Note: In orbit, gravity continuously pulls the satellite towards Earth, bending its path into a closed orbit.

Set 14 | Q.No 26 | Topic: Science & Technology | Language: English
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Q: यदि चंद्रमा को पृथ्वी की परिक्रमा करने में 27 दिन लगते हैं, तो वह अपनी कक्षा में प्रतिदिन कितने डिग्री घूमता है?
   A) 13.3 degrees  <-- CORRECT
   B) 27 degrees
   C) 360 degrees
   D) 7 degrees
Answer: A
Why correct: If the Moon completes its orbit (360 degrees) in about 27 days, it moves roughly 360/27 = 13.3 degrees per day.
Why B is wrong: 27 degrees is the number of days, not the daily angular motion.
Why C is wrong: 360 degrees is the full orbit, covered over the whole 27 days.
Why D is wrong: 7 degrees per day would imply an orbit much slower than 27 days.
Note: This daily shift is why the Moon rises roughly 50 minutes later each day.

Set 15 | Q.No 25 | Topic: Science & Technology | Language: Hindi
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Q: पृथ्वी और चंद्रमा के बीच औसत दूरी 384,000 किमी है। चंद्रमा का व्यास लगभग 3,474 किमी है। पृथ्वी से देखे गए चंद्रमा के कोणीय व्यास का परिकलन (रेडियन में) कीजिए।
   A) 0.009 रेडियन  <-- CORRECT
   B) 0.008 रेडियन
   C) 0.010 ¢fsaq
   D) 0.007 रेडियन
Answer: A
Why correct: Angular diameter (in radians) = actual diameter / distance = 3,474 / 384,000 = about 0.009 radian.
Why B is wrong: 0.008 radian is slightly too small for this calculation.
Why C is wrong: 0.010 radian is a little too large.
Why D is wrong: 0.007 radian is too small.
Note: This tiny angular size (about half a degree) is why the Moon and Sun appear almost the same size in our sky.

Set 15 | Q.No 26 | Topic: Science & Technology | Language: Hindi
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Q: 300 किमी की ऊंचाई पर, किसी उपग्रह की कक्षीय चाल 7.8 किमी/सेकंड है। यदि उपग्रह की ऊंचाई में 200 किमी की वृद्धि होती है, तो उसकी कक्षीय अवधि पर क्या प्रभाव पड़ेगा?
   A) इसमें वृद्धि होगी  <-- CORRECT
   B) इसमें कमी होगी
   C) कोई परिवर्तन नहीं होगा
   D) यादृच्छिक रूप से बदलता रहेगा
Answer: A
Why correct: If a satellite's altitude increases, its orbital radius grows, so its orbital period increases (by Kepler's third law, a larger orbit takes longer).
Why B is wrong: The period increases, not decreases, with greater altitude.
Why C is wrong: There is a definite change; it does not stay the same.
Why D is wrong: The change is systematic (an increase), not random.
Note: Higher orbits are slower: a satellite farther from Earth travels at a lower speed and takes longer per revolution.

Set 15 | Q.No 27 | Topic: Science & Technology | Language: Hindi
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Q: 65।/ ।त ॥॥ (/५3) की ८0 तक 4000 0 पेलोड क्षमता है। यदि यह 3600 ४0 का उपग्रह लॉन्च करता है, और दक्षता 90% है, तो वास्तविक ऊर्जा आदर्श ऊर्जा की तुलना में कितनी उपयोग की गई है ?
   A) 1.1 times  <-- CORRECT
   B) 1.2 times
   C) 1.0 times
   D) 0.9 times
Answer: A
Why correct: With 90% efficiency, the actual energy used is the ideal energy divided by 0.9, i.e. about 1.1 times the ideal energy (more input is needed to account for losses).
Why B is wrong: 1.2 times would correspond to about 83% efficiency.
Why C is wrong: 1.0 times would mean 100% efficiency (no losses).
Why D is wrong: 0.9 times would wrongly imply less energy than ideal is used.
Note: Efficiency = useful output / total input, so lower efficiency means more input energy is required.

   A) प्रदूषण प्रभावित क्षेत्र
   B) खनन क्षेत्र
   C) वन्यजीव गलियारे
   D) संरक्षित क्षेत्रों के आसपास के बफर जोन  <-- CORRECT
Answer: D
Why correct: An 'Eco-Sensitive Zone' (ESZ) is a buffer zone around protected areas (national parks and wildlife sanctuaries) where harmful activities are regulated.
Why A is wrong: It is not simply a pollution-affected area.
Why B is wrong: It is not a mining zone; mining is restricted there.
Why C is wrong: Wildlife corridors are related but the ESZ specifically refers to buffer zones around protected areas.
Note: ESZs act as 'shock absorbers' for protected areas, with graded restrictions on industry and construction.

Set 15 | Q.No 40 | Topic: Science & Technology | Language: Hindi
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Q: धारा प्रवाहित करने वाला एक आयताकार लूप किसी चुंबकीय क्षेत्र में स्वतंत्र रूप से लटका हुआ है। यह स्वाभाविक रूप से किस स्थिति में पहुँचेगा?
   A) क्षेत्र रेखाओं के लंबवत
   B) यादृच्छिक अभिविन्यास
   C) क्षेत्र रेखाओं के समानांतर  <-- CORRECT
   D) कोई निश्चित स्थिति नहीं है
Answer: C
Why correct: A freely suspended current-carrying rectangular loop in a magnetic field rotates until its plane lies along (parallel to) the field lines - i.e. its magnetic moment aligns with the field - which is its stable equilibrium.
Why A is wrong: With its plane perpendicular to the field lines the loop experiences maximum torque, so it does not stay there.
Why B is wrong: It settles into a definite orientation, not a random one.
Why D is wrong: There is a definite stable position, contrary to this option.
Note: This aligning torque on a current loop is the basic principle behind moving-coil galvanometers and electric motors.

Q: Which constitutional body audits the accounts of the Union and states?
   A) Finance Commission
   B) Comptroller and Auditor General  <-- CORRECT
   C) NITI Aayog
   D) Union Public Service Commission
Answer: B
Why correct: The Comptroller and Auditor General (CAG) of India is the constitutional authority (Article 148) that audits the accounts of the Union and the state governments.
Why A is wrong: The Finance Commission recommends tax sharing, it does not audit accounts.
Why C is wrong: NITI Aayog is a policy think-tank, not an auditor.
Why D is wrong: The UPSC conducts recruitment exams for the civil services.
Note: The CAG is often called the guardian of the public purse; its reports are examined by the Public Accounts Committee.

Set 16 | Q.No 22 | Topic: Polity & Constitution | Language: English
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Q: Which type of emergency has never been proclaimed in India?
   A) National Emergency
   B) President’s Rule
   C) Financial Emergency  <-- CORRECT
   D) None of the above
Answer: C
Why correct: A Financial Emergency (Article 360) has never been proclaimed in India.
Why A is wrong: National Emergency (Article 352) has been declared (e.g. 1962, 1971, 1975).
Why B is wrong: President's Rule (Article 356) has been used many times in the states.
Why D is wrong: 'None of the above' is wrong because the Financial Emergency is the one never used.
Note: The closest India came to a financial crisis without Article 360 was the 1991 balance-of-payments crisis.

   B) State Legislature
   C) Governor  <-- CORRECT
   D) President
Answer: C

Why A is wrong: The Chief Minister advises but does not formally appoint the Advocate General.
Why B is wrong: The State Legislature has no appointing power here.
Why D is wrong: The President appoints the Attorney General for the Union, not the state's Advocate General.
Note: The Advocate General is the state-level equivalent of the Attorney General of India.

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Q: What is the frequency range of sound that can be heard by the human ear?
   A) 2 Hz to 200 Hz
   B) 20 Hz to 20,000 Hz  <-- CORRECT
   C) 200 Hz to 2000 Hz
   D) 2000 Hz to 20,000 Hz
Answer: B
Why correct: The human ear can hear sound in the frequency range of about 20 Hz to 20,000 Hz (20 kHz).
Why A is wrong: 2-200 Hz is far below the full audible range.
Why C is wrong: 200-2000 Hz is only a part of the audible range.
Why D is wrong: 2000-20,000 Hz covers only the higher part of the range.
Note: Sound below 20 Hz is called infrasound and above 20 kHz is ultrasound.

Why A is wrong: 'The Excursion' is a long poem by Wordsworth.
Why B is wrong: 'Intimations of Immortality' is a famous ode by Wordsworth.
Why D is wrong: 'Michael' is a pastoral poem by Wordsworth.

Q: Which of the following is the largest contributor to urban PM2.5 in India?
   A) industrial emissions
   B) Construction dust
   C) Vehicle exhaust
   D) All of these  <-- CORRECT
Answer: D
Why correct: Urban PM2.5 in India comes from several major sources together - industrial emissions, construction dust and vehicle exhaust - so 'all of these' is correct.
Why A is wrong: Industrial emissions are one source but not the only one.
Why B is wrong: Construction dust is significant but not the sole contributor.
Why C is wrong: Vehicle exhaust is major but combined with the others.
Note: PM2.5 refers to fine particles under 2.5 micrometres that penetrate deep into the lungs.

Set 16 | Q.No 27 | Topic: Geography | Language: English
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Q: Which of the following meteorological factors can reduce Air Quality Index (AQI) temporarily?
   A) High humidity without rain
   B) Calm wind
   C) Temperature inversion
   D) Rain  <-- CORRECT
Answer: D
Why correct: Rain temporarily improves air quality (lowers AQI) by washing pollutants and dust out of the air.
Why A is wrong: High humidity without rain can trap pollutants and worsen AQI.
Why B is wrong: Calm wind allows pollutants to accumulate, raising AQI.
Why C is wrong: Temperature inversion traps pollutants near the ground, worsening AQI.
Note: A higher AQI value means worse air; rain causes 'wet deposition' of particulate matter.

   B) iodine  <-- CORRECT
   C) Sodium
   D) Potassium
Answer: B

Why A is wrong: Calcium is needed for bones and is regulated by other hormones.
Why C is wrong: Sodium is an electrolyte, not the element in thyroxine.
Why D is wrong: Potassium is an electrolyte, not used to make thyroxine.
Note: Iodine deficiency causes goitre; iodised salt is used to prevent it.

Set 16 | Q.No 39 | Topic: Economy | Language: English
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Q: Which of the following is NOT the way to finance a budgetary deficit? I. Borrowings II. Taxation
   A) Only I
   B) Only II
   C) Both I and II
   D) Neither I nor II  <-- CORRECT
Answer: D
Why correct: Both borrowings (I) and taxation (II) are legitimate ways by which a government finances its expenditure and bridges a budgetary gap, so neither is excluded - hence 'Neither I nor II'.
Why A is wrong: 'Only I' wrongly excludes taxation as a source of finance.
Why B is wrong: 'Only II' wrongly excludes borrowings.
Why C is wrong: 'Both I and II' would mean both are NOT ways, which is incorrect.
Note: A government typically meets its spending through tax revenue, non-tax revenue and borrowings.

Set 17 | Q.No 21 | Topic: Geography | Language: Hindi
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Q: निम्नलिखित में से कौन-सा वह साधन नहीं है, जिससे भूमिगत जल सतह तक पहुंचता है?
   A) झरनों के माध्यम से
   B) कुओं के माध्यम से
   C) नलकूप के माध्यम से
   D) वाष्पीकरण के माध्यम से  <-- CORRECT
Answer: D
Why correct: Evaporation removes water from the surface into the air; it is NOT a way by which underground water reaches the surface.
Why A is wrong: Springs are a natural way groundwater emerges at the surface.
Why B is wrong: Wells bring groundwater up to the surface.
Why C is wrong: Tube wells pump groundwater to the surface.
Note: Springs, wells and tube wells all tap the water table, whereas evaporation is part of the loss side of the water cycle.

Set 17 | Q.No 25 | Topic: Science & Technology | Language: Hindi

Q: यदि चंद्रमा, पृथ्वी की सतह पर 0.5" का कोण अंतरित करता है, तो इसके व्यास का परिकलन कीजिए, दिया गया है कि पृथ्वी से इसकी औसत दूरी 3.8:«0” मीटर है।
   A) 3500 किमी
   B) 3475 किमी  <-- CORRECT
   C) 3000 किमी
   D) 4000 किमी
Answer: B
Why correct: Using diameter = angular size (in radians) x distance: 0.5 degrees is about 0.0087 rad; 0.0087 x 3.8x10^8 m gives roughly 3,475 km, the Moon's diameter.
Why A is wrong: 3500 km is close but the precise value is about 3,475 km.
Why C is wrong: 3000 km is too small.
Why D is wrong: 4000 km is too large.
Note: The Moon's actual diameter is about 3,474 km, roughly a quarter of Earth's.

   B) मंगल और बृहस्पति के बीच क्षुद्रग्रह घेरा है
   C) धूमकेतु की पूंछ है
   D) सूर्य के चारों ओर का वह क्षेत्र है जो सौर पवन उत्पन्न करता है

Set 17 | Q.No 27 | Topic: Science & Technology | Language: Hindi

Q: किस भारतीय मिशन ने भारत को अपने पहले प्रयास में ही मंगल की कक्षा में सफलतापूर्वक पहुंचने वाला पहला देश बना दिया?
   A) PSLV-1
   B) Mangalyaan (MOM)  <-- CORRECT
   C) Chandrayaan-2
   D) Aditya-L1
Answer: B
Why correct: The Mars Orbiter Mission (Mangalyaan) made India the first country to reach Mars orbit on its very first attempt (2014).
Why A is wrong: The PSLV is a launch vehicle, not the Mars mission itself.
Why C is wrong: Chandrayaan-2 was a lunar mission.
Why D is wrong: Aditya-L1 is India's solar mission.
Note: Mangalyaan was also one of the most cost-effective interplanetary missions ever flown.

Set 17 | Q.No 35 | Topic: Science & Technology | Language: Hindi
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Q: एक आवेशित कण एकसमान चुंबकीय क्षेत्र में क्षेत्र के लंबवत वेग से प्रवेश करता है। इसकी गति की प्रकृति क्या है?
   A) सीधी रेखा
   B) वृत्ताकार पथ  <-- CORRECT
   C) कुंडलित पथ
   D) यादृच्छिक गति
Answer: B
Why correct: A charged particle entering a uniform magnetic field perpendicular to it moves in a circular path, because the magnetic force always acts perpendicular to its velocity.
Why A is wrong: It does not move in a straight line; a force acts on it.
Why C is wrong: A helical (spiral) path occurs when the velocity has a component along the field, not perpendicular.
Why D is wrong: The motion is well-defined (circular), not random.
Note: This circular motion is the basis of devices like the cyclotron.

Set 17 | Q.No 36 | Topic: History | Language: Hindi

Q: मुगल साम्राज्य के अंतर्गत ज़ब्त प्रणाली गुजरात तथा बंगाल जैसे प्रांतों में क्यों लागू नहीं की गई थी?
   A) मिट्टी की खराब गुणवत्ता
   B) लगातार विदेशी आक्रमण
   C) भूमि का निरीक्षण करने में असमर्थता  <-- CORRECT
   D) स्थानीय प्रशासन की कमी
Answer: C
Why correct: The Zabt revenue system was not applied in provinces like Gujarat and Bengal mainly because of the inability to survey and measure the land accurately there.
Why A is wrong: Poor soil quality was not the reason for skipping Zabt.
Why B is wrong: Continuous foreign invasions were not the cause.
Why D is wrong: It was not due to a lack of local administration as such, but the difficulty of land measurement.
Note: The Zabt system, developed under Akbar (Todar Mal), fixed revenue based on measured land and average yields.

Set 17 | Q.No 40 | Topic: Sports | Language: Hindi

Q: टेनिस में, जब कोई खिलाड़ी गेंद को नेट के ठीक ऊपर तथा विपरीत दिशा में गिराने के लिए अपने शॉट की गति कम कर देता है, तो इसे कहा जाता हैं।
   A) ड्रॉप शॉट  <-- CORRECT
   B) स्मैश
   C) स्लाइस
   D) टू-हैण्ड

   C) 52वां संशोधन

Q: अप्रैल 2025 में, सिकल सेल रोग (एस.सी.डी) की प्रारंभिक जांच के लिए एक किफायती इलेक्ट्रो-फुइडडिक उपकरण किस भारतीय अनुसंधान संस्थान द्वारा विकसित किया गया था?
   A) टाटा मेमोरियल सेंटर
   B) रमन अनुसंधान संस्थान  <-- CORRECT
   C) वैज्ञानिक और औद्योगिक अनुसंधान परिषद
   D) अखिल भारतीय आयुर्विज्ञान संस्थान
Answer: B
Why correct: In April 2025, the Raman Research Institute developed an affordable electro-fluidic device for the early screening of Sickle Cell Disease (SCD).
Why A is wrong: Tata Memorial Centre focuses on cancer care, not this device.
Why C is wrong: CSIR is a broad research body, but the device was credited to the Raman Research Institute.
Why D is wrong: AIIMS is a medical institute but not the developer cited here.
Note: India runs a National Sickle Cell Anaemia Elimination Mission targeting tribal and vulnerable populations.

Set 19 | Q.No 40 | Topic: Sports | Language: Hindi
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Q: टेनिस मैच में निम्नलिखित में से कौन सा शॉट खेला जाता है? [. फोरहैंड [. बैकहैंड
   A) Only I
   B) Only II
   C) Both I and II  <-- CORRECT
   D) Neither I nor II
Answer: C
Why correct: Both the forehand (I) and the backhand (II) are standard groundstrokes played in a tennis match, so 'Both I and II' is correct.
Why A is wrong: 'Only I' leaves out the backhand.
Why B is wrong: 'Only II' leaves out the forehand.
Why D is wrong: 'Neither' is wrong since both are common tennis shots.
Note: Other tennis strokes include the serve, volley, smash and drop shot.

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Q: लोकसभा का चुनाव लड़ने के लिए न्यूनतम आयु है :
   A) 18 years
   B) 21 years
   C) 25 years  <-- CORRECT
   D) 30 years
Answer: C
Why correct: The minimum age to contest a Lok Sabha election is 25 years.
Why A is wrong: 18 years is the minimum voting age, not the age to contest.
Why B is wrong: 21 years is not the qualifying age for the Lok Sabha.
Why D is wrong: 30 years is the minimum age to become a member of the Rajya Sabha.
Note: For the Rajya Sabha the minimum age is 30; for the Lok Sabha and Legislative Assembly it is 25.

   B) वैज्ञानिक और औद्योगिक अनुसंधान परिषद
   C) राज्य संदर्भ संगठन

   A) मृदा प्रदूषण कम करना
   B) जल प्रदूषण की निगरानी करना
   C) आगामी उच्च प्रदूषण वाले दिनों के बारे में नागरिकों को सचेत करना  <-- CORRECT

   A) घ्राण ग्राही  <-- CORRECT

Set 20 | Q.No 31 | Topic: History | Language: Hindi
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Q: सल्तनत के अधीन इक्‍्ता प्रणाली मध्ययुगीन यूरोप की सामंती प्रणाली से मुख्यतः: इसलिए मिलती जुलती है क्योंकि ।
   A) दोनों में भूमि के वंशानुगत हस्तांतरण की अनुमति दी जाती है
   B) दोनों को राजस्व अधिकारों के बदले सैन्य सेवा के लिए डिज़ाइन किया गया था  <-- CORRECT
   C) दोनों व्यापारिक एकाधिकार थे
   D) दोनों व्यापारियों पर लागू होने वाली कराधान की प्रणालियाँ थीं
Answer: B
Why correct: The Iqta system under the Delhi Sultanate resembled European feudalism mainly because both granted revenue rights (over land) in return for military service.
Why A is wrong: The Iqta was not originally hereditary, unlike much European feudal land.
Why C is wrong: Neither was a trade monopoly.
Why D is wrong: They were not merely taxation systems on merchants.
Note: An 'iqtadar' (or muqti) collected revenue from his iqta and maintained troops for the Sultan.

Q: किस अधिनियम ने पहली बार भारतीयों को केन्द्रीय विधान सभा में प्रतिनिधित्व दिया?
   A) Indian Councils Act, 1861
   B) Indian Councils Act, 1892
   C) Indian Councils Act, 1909  <-- CORRECT
   D) Government of India Act, 1919
Answer: C
Why correct: The Indian Councils Act, 1909 (Morley-Minto Reforms) gave Indians a measure of representation in the central legislature for the first time.
Why A is wrong: The 1861 Act allowed only nominated non-officials.
Why B is wrong: The 1892 Act expanded councils but is not credited with this representation milestone.
Why D is wrong: The 1919 Act came later.
Note: The 1909 Act also introduced separate electorates for Muslims, a controversial step.

Set 20 | Q.No 36 | Topic: Science & Technology | Language: Hindi
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Q: जब पराध्वानी तरंगों को सफाई के विलयन में भेजा जाता है तो धूल, चिकनाई तथा गंदगी के कणों का क्या होता हैं?
   A) वे वाष्पित हो जाते हैं
   B) वे घुल जाते हैं
   C) वे अलग होकर निचे गिर जाते हैं  <-- CORRECT
   D) वे जल जाते हैं
Answer: C
Why correct: When ultrasonic (ultrasound) waves are passed through a cleaning solution, the vibration shakes loose dust, grease and dirt particles, which separate and fall away from the object.
Why A is wrong: They do not evaporate.
Why B is wrong: They do not dissolve.
Why D is wrong: They are not burnt off.
Note: Ultrasonic cleaning works through 'cavitation' - tiny bubbles that scrub surfaces clean.

   A) Only I  <-- CORRECT
   B) Only II
   C) Both I and II
   D) Neither I nor II

Why correct: According to Census 2011, the Jain community (I) is the most urbanised religious group in India, largely concentrated in urban areas; Christians (II) are not predominantly urban.

Set 20 | Q.No 38 | Topic: Economy | Language: Hindi
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Q: एक निश्चित विनिमय दर प्रणाली में, जब किसी सरकारी कार्रवाई द्वारा विनिमय दर बढ़ाती हैं, तो इसे कहा जाता है, जिससे घरेलू मुद्रा सस्ती हो जाती हैं।
   A) मूल्यहास
   B) मूल्यवृद्धि
   C) अवमूल्यन  <-- CORRECT
   D) पुर्गमूल्यन
Answer: C
Why correct: Under a fixed exchange-rate system, when the government officially raises the exchange rate so that the domestic currency becomes cheaper, it is called devaluation.
Why A is wrong: Depreciation is a fall in a currency's value under a floating system, not a deliberate official act under a fixed system.
Why B is wrong: Appreciation is a rise in currency value.
Why D is wrong: Revaluation is an official increase in the currency's value (the opposite of devaluation).
Note: India devalued the rupee in 1966 and again sharply in 1991.

   A) विश्व व्यापार संगठन
   B) अंतर्राष्ट्रीय न्यायालय
   C) अंतर्री्ट्रीय सौर गठबंधन  <-- CORRECT
   D) सार्क
Answer: C
